<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рекомендоваться.html>рекомендова́ться</a> (7046)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рекомендовать.html>рекомендова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rekomendovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рекомендоваться.html>рекомендова́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rekomendovátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">порекомендова́ться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to introduce oneself</li>
<li>to be advisable/recommended (+ infinitive)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:рекомендоваться.html>рекоменду́ется</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rekomendújetsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">it is advisable/recommended (that + clause)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:такой.html>тако́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:способ.html>спо́соб</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:рекомендоваться.html>рекоменд́уется</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">takój spósob ne <b>rekomend́ujetsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">this method is not advisable/recommended</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:такой.html>тако́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:случай.html>слу́чае</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:рекомендоваться.html>рекоменду́ется</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:следующий.html>сле́дующее</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v takóm slúčaje <b>rekomendújetsja</b> slédujuščeje</i> ― <span class="e-translation">in this case the following is recommended</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рекомендовать.html>рекомендова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rekomendovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рекомендовать.html>рекомендова́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rekomendovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порекомендовать.html>порекомендова́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">porekomendovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:реконструкция.html>реконстру́кция</a> (7792)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реконструкция.html>реконстру́кция</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rekonstrúkcija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реконструкция.html>реконстру́кции</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реконструкция.html>реконстру́кции</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реконструкция.html>реконстру́кций</a></b>)

***ремень.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ремень.html>реме́нь</a> (2117)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*remy</i> (genitive <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*remene</i>). Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">ремыкъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">remykŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu"><a href = vnd.unilang:ремень.html>реме́нь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">remenĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">ремінь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">reminʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; Bulgarian <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">ремен</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">remen</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">ремик</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">remik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">ремък</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">remǎk</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; Serbo-Croatian <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">ре̏ме̑н</i> (genitive <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">ремена</i>), <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">рѐмик</i>; Slovenian <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">rémen</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">jérmen</i>; Czech <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">řemen</i>, Slovak <i class="Latn mention" lang="sk">remeň</i>; Polish <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">rzemień</i>; <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Upper_Sorbian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Upper Sorbian language">Upper Sorbian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="hsb">rjemjeń</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lower_Sorbian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lower Sorbian language">Lower Sorbian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dsb">rjemjeń</i>.
</p><p>Despite the similarity to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Riemen</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">riomо</i>), Vasmer concludes that the claim of some earlier dictionaries that the Slavic word is a loan of the Germanic one is phonologically impossible; see <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Riemen</i> for more.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ремень.html>реме́нь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">reménʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ремень.html>ремня́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ремень.html>ремни́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ремень.html>ремне́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>strap, thong, sling</li>
<li>belt, waist-belt</li></ol>

***ремесло.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ремесло.html>ремесло́</a> (7256)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology is missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ремесло.html>ремесло́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">remesló</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ремесло.html>ремесла́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ремесло.html>ремёсла</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ремесло.html>ремёсел</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>trade, craft <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">skilled practice</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>handicraft</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> profession, occupation</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> uncreative work, unimaginative work, work according to a template</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ремень.html>реме́нь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">reménʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-шо́к</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-šók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ремешок.html>ремешо́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">remešók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ремешок.html>ремешка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ремешок.html>ремешки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ремешок.html>ремешко́в</a></b>)

***ремонт.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ремонт.html>ремо́нт</a> (3194)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">remonter</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ремонт.html>ремо́нт</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">remónt</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ремонт.html>ремо́нта</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ремонт.html>ремо́нты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ремонт.html>ремо́нтов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>repair, overhaul</li>
<li>maintenance</li>
<li>mending, renovation, refurbishment</li>
<li>refit</li>
<li>remount service</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ремонтировать.html>ремонти́ровать</a> (10559)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***ренессанс.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ренессанс.html>ренесса́нс</a> (23722)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">Renaissance</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ренессанс.html>ренесса́нс</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rɛnɛssáns, renessáns</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ренессанс.html>ренесса́нса</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ренессанс.html>ренесса́нсы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ренессанс.html>ренесса́нсов</a></b>)
